    "uuid": "4bfb2be7-30ee-463c-9e87-adc8258b5879",
    "post_id": 1066,
    "type": "blogs",
    "title": "Transforming supply chains and the talent gap",
    "slug": "transforming-supply-chains-and-the-talent-gap",
    "date": "2019-05-29T16:48:19",
    "summary": null,
    "main_points": null,
    "recent_news": null,
    "related_articles": [],
    "web_content": "<p><img fetchpriority=\"high\" decoding=\"async\" class=\"size-medium wp-image-1068 alignleft\" src=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Supply-chain-new-article-May-2019-300x219.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"300\" height=\"219\" title=\"\" srcset=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Supply-chain-new-article-May-2019-300x219.jpg 300w, https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Supply-chain-new-article-May-2019-600x439.jpg 600w, https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Supply-chain-new-article-May-2019-768x562.jpg 768w, https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/Supply-chain-new-article-May-2019.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" /></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Global supply chains are changing rapidly and many businesses are recognizing that adopting new technology will help them navigate the changes, streamline their operations, and save time and money. With the pressure to apply technological solutions to get ahead of the game, businesses of all sizes are also facing a widening supply chain talent gap.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Investment in </span><a href=\"http://www.tradeready.ca/2019/topics/supply-chain-management/do-you-need-to-digitally-transform-your-supply-chain/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">supply chain</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> digitization is accelerating rapidly. Better demand planning, product traceability, real-time product visibility, and anomaly detection are some examples of using data in new ways &#8211; and while it can be a game changer, it comes at a cost.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">At the same time, research shows that while there is a growing understanding of the need to digitally transform their supply chains, many organizations struggle to implement them.</span></p>\n<p><b>Transforming supply chains with technology</b></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The process to re-engineer, streamline and apply technology to transform </span><a href=\"http://www.tradeready.ca/2018/topics/supply-chain-management/how-your-company-can-use-automation-today-to-improve-supply-chain-management-efficiency/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">supply chains</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is complex. &#8220;Lags with supply chain transformation has a lot to do with hurdles that arise with any large-scale change&#8221; – challenges with budget, lack of organizational urgency, and implementation of new technology into legacy systems, according to an </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">industry whitepaper report</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> by Avetta.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Investing in the right technology and the resources to implement is further complicated by the rate of change in the supply chain environment, as well as increasing supply chain disruptions and risks.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Avetta&#8217;s whitepaper adds that &#8220;changing workplace safety and labour laws, constantly shifting geopolitical dynamics, and unpredictability in prices continue to impact risk and vendor management&#8230;. inconsistent vendor on-boarding, delayed shipments, and inefficient inventory management are common bottlenecks.”</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Digitizing the </span><a href=\"https://fittfortrade.com/global-value-chain\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">supply chain</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> seems to be the key to increasing transparency and visibility while controlling replenishment, maintenance, production, transportation, delivery and customer satisfaction, as well as driving efficiencies and mitigating risk. Automation and artificial intelligence (AI) technology is unlocking real-time decision making and forecasts. Big data and predictive analytics can provide new levels of transparency and increased cost savings.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">With each advancement in technology, the way companies do business internally, and with each other is changing and it’s profoundly changing the supply chain management labour market.</span></p>\n<p><b>The supply chain talent gap</b></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Labour shortages in the supply chain industry are well documented. According to a report by </span><a href=\"https://www.datexcorp.com/labor-shortages-in-the-supply-chain-workforce/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Datex</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">; &#8220;Growing complexity of the supply chain is also negatively impacting the available labor pool. Customer needs and requirements are increasing in areas such as order fulfillment, VAS and omni-channel retailing. This increase in complexity means workers must have more technical skills to fulfill minimum requirements&#8230; 60% of supply chain jobs require skills that a mere 20% of the labor pool possesses.&#8221;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The projections indicate that it&#8217;s a situation that is not going to get resolved any time soon. “For every graduate with supply chain skills there are six holes to be filled, and it could be as high as nine to one in the future,” </span><a href=\"https://www.supplychain247.com/paper/the_supply_chain_talent_shortage_from_gap_to_crisis/apics\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">warns Jake Barr, CEO of BlueWorld Supply Chain Consulting.</span></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The labor shortage in the supply chain workforce is affecting businesses worldwide. Companies have a lot at stake when hiring someone to handle these large and ever-changing supply chains, as </span><a href=\"http://www.tradeready.ca/2015/trade-takeaways/falling-behind-technology-transforms-supply-chain-recruitment/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Denise Montrose</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> points out. Beyond recruitment, what&#8217;s the best strategy for </span><a href=\"http://www.tradeready.ca/2015/trade-takeaways/we-need-to-stop-passing-up-new-grads-and-develop-talented-candidates-in-the-supply-chain-industry/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">empowering your employees</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> who are dealing with the complexity and the challenges on the day-to-day? &#8220;How fast can you change direction with a new system, software, or tool and expect the team to keep up?&#8221;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Leading companies are </span><a href=\"https://www.supplychain247.com/paper/the_supply_chain_talent_shortage_from_gap_to_crisis/apics\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">actively working on the shortage problem</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. The solution begins with developing their workforce through clear career-pathing, education, talent development partnerships and other means.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cisco Systems’ SVP of Supply Chain Operations, John Kern, recently said “The supply chain industry is undergoing one of the most massive talent shifts we have ever seen.”</span></p>\n<p><b>Train for the new supply chain landscape</b></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.tradeready.ca/2015/trade-takeaways/falling-behind-technology-transforms-supply-chain-recruitment/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you are looking to have a future in SCM</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, then you need to be smart, fast, flexible, engaged, intuitive, and above all else analytical. It&#8217;s a highly technical landscape requiring a new suite of skills. Preparing for the brave new world of supply chain management will require real life hands-on training, Denise Montrose explains.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&#8220;When considering a university program, think about how well prepared you will be at graduation. Academic education can only get you so far. Hands-on training, internships, field trips, and real world experience&#8230;will provide you the </span><a href=\"http://www.tradeready.ca/2015/trade-takeaways/falling-behind-technology-transforms-supply-chain-recruitment/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">best start to a promising career</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Students need to dive in and get their hands dirty. They must have the ability to multitask, change direction with flexibility, and they must possess the discipline to ask questions until they find the right answers. They need to think for themselves under great pressure and analyze solutions.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For those already engaged in the industry, a key piece of advice is to develop your knowledge and skills with the technology being used within your organization, as well as in the industry. </span><a href=\"http://www.tradeready.ca/2015/trade-takeaways/falling-behind-technology-transforms-supply-chain-recruitment/\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Beyond staying current with technology</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, Denise Montrose points out that &#8220;certifications are a great way to ensure that you are still learning about industry trends.&#8221;</span></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://goto.fittfortrade.com/fitt-small-business-guide-scaling-up/?utm_source=promopartner&amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;utm_campaign=letstalksupplychain\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><img decoding=\"async\" class=\"size-medium wp-image-1071 aligncenter\" src=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/FITT-Small-Business-Guide-The-Scaling-Up-Edition-500-width-300x148.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"300\" height=\"148\" title=\"\" srcset=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/FITT-Small-Business-Guide-The-Scaling-Up-Edition-500-width-300x148.jpg 300w, https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/FITT-Small-Business-Guide-The-Scaling-Up-Edition-500-width.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" /></a></p>\n",

    "uuid": "421bd112-97b5-4a11-8ed9-67640f70d63b",
    "post_id": 654,
    "type": "blogs",
    "title": "3 Amazon Moves You Need to Know About Now and How You Can Compete",
    "slug": "3-amazon-moves-you-need-to-know-about-now-and-how-you-can-compete",
    "date": "2019-05-15T23:39:21",
    "summary": null,
    "main_points": null,
    "recent_news": null,
    "related_articles": [],
    "web_content": "<p>Amazon is fundamentally changing the way consumers and industry professionals think about retail and supply chain. And, if you’re reading this then you probably already realize that when it comes to supply chain and commerce – change is the only constant now. The industry is moving harder and faster to reach escalating customer demands fueled by the eCommerce giant and on demand technologies.</p>\n<p>So, how did we get here and how do we move forward?</p>\n<p>Supply chain’s digital age was started by advancements in technology and the generation that now occupies the largest consumer spending block: millennials. The consumer buyer’s cycle has become a blip and on demand services and mobile means businesses have a captive audience of shoppers all the time, everywhere and they want everything now.</p>\n<p>If it seems like your news and social feeds are saturated by the eCommerce leader and their every next move – that’s because they are. But by monitoring Amazon’s progress, retailers, manufacturers and logistics providers across the chain can see what’s next in digital and how to elevate their strategies.</p>\n<p>To make it convenient for you, here are the 3 latest Amazon moves you can’t miss and how you can respond:</p>\n<p>1. Prime members now get same-day and one-day deliveries in select areas.</p>\n<p>Think Uber, but for Amazon. Amazon has been building a national presence of distribution centers, backed by full-time drivers and the gig economy. Amazon Flex drivers <a href=\"https://flex.amazon.com/\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">make $18-25 hourly with the autonomy</a> of being their own bosses. If a driver is 21 or over and has a mid-sized sedan or truck and current driver’s license they are directed to the app and ready to go. These drivers give Amazon edge for last-mile deliveries to keep one-day and same-day deliveries on schedule.</p>\n<p><img fetchpriority=\"high\" decoding=\"async\" class=\"alignright\" style=\"text-align: right;\" src=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/LTSC-3-Amazon-Moves-You-Need-to-Know-About-Now-and-How-You-Can-Compete.jpg\" width=\"362\" height=\"241\" alt=\"\" title=\"\"></p>\n<p>While consumers are all in for quick deliveries, one <a href=\"https://twitter.com/GaleBonker/status/1122882620423954432\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">tweeted</a>, “Please stop,” linking an article on union’s raising concerns for warehouse workers. “Humanity doesn’t need this.” Speaking of humanity, last year Business Insider released a disturbing report on Amazon’s working conditions from the company’s drivers&#8217; first-hand, revealing the “true cost of free shipping”.</p>\n<p>While consumers are all in for quick deliveries, one tweeted, “Please stop,” linking an article on union’s raising concerns for warehouse workers. “Humanity doesn’t need this.” Speaking of humanity, last year Business Insider <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-delivery-drivers-reveal-claims-of-disturbing-work-conditions-2018-8\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">released a disturbing report</a> on Amazon’s working conditions from the company’s drivers&#8217; first-hand, revealing the “true cost of free shipping”.</p>\n<div style=\"font-weight: bold;\">\n<p>How can you compete? While our on demand economy mandates the right technologies, retailers and their partners across the supply chain need to think bigger than that. Some retailers are already offering in-store and curb-side pickup; why not add same-day deliveries to that list? While more retailers are already offering delivery, none are amassing the gig economy drivers the way Amazon is. Why not?</p>\n<p>Isn’t it time for retailers to take the same approach in building out an on demand fleet of flexible drivers? If your business isn’t talking about having a Chief on Demand Officer (CODO), you probably should—soon. There is no reason retail chains and logistics companies can’t build out a network of on demand drivers like Amazon has for local and last-mile, same and next-day deliveries. Or, look for ways to tap into partnerships with Lyft and Uber, companies known for their entrepreneurialism, growing partnerships and endless innovation.</p>\n<p>And why not be competitive with Amazon when it comes to getting truckers and warehouse workers and tap into social sentiment that’s reached the upper echelons of American democracy? There is a shortage of truckers and warehouse labor for retailers, 3PLS and logistics companies to hire – push the benefits of working for your business.</p>\n<p>Focus on the human element and the working conditions that align with your company’s values and their unions’. Partner with unions in getting your message out – Amazon isn’t just competing for shoppers they’re also competing for the workforce that make their service levels possible.</p>\n<p>And don’t stop there. <a href=\"https://nrf.com/blog/connecting-socially-aware-consumers\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">According to the National Retail Federation (NRF)</a> millennials want to shop from socially conscious brands that align with their values. In fact, the federation shared that around 60% of consumers would ditch their favorite brands if they realized the business’s values don’t align with their own. Make sure your brand is promoting in your marketing, on your website, social media and in the media how you value your employee experience as much as your customer experience – it matters.</p>\n<p>2. Some retailers are now taking Amazon returns.</p>\n<p>In fact, <a href=\"https://www.kohls.com/feature/amazon.jsp\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Kohl’s is now accepting and shipping</a> returns for shoppers for free. The move will bring the national retail chain more foot traffic and empower them to find opportunities to help shoppers find similar items right inside of their stores. While an interesting concept, it’s a double-edged sword.</p>\n<p><img decoding=\"async\" class=\"alignleft\" style=\"text-align: left;\" src=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/LTSC-3-Amazon-Moves-You-Need-to-Know-About-Now-and-How-You-Can-Compete-2.png\" width=\"386\" height=\"255\" alt=\"\" title=\"\"></p>\n<p>How can you compete? Retailers can be focusing on making returns easier for their eCommerce purchases by ensuring all returns can be accepted right in the store. Retailers should be pushing this message out to the masses – if you don’t love it, bring it to your nearest location and exchange it for something you do or get your money back.</p>\n<p>Sound basic, maybe a little old school? Exactly. That’s because it is. While technology and convenience have been reshaping the industry landscape across the supply chain, there are some mainstays inherent to marketing that haven’t changed – creating a positive, personal customer experience. And sometimes driving to the closest store to exchange that jacket you need for tomorrow’s interview is a better option than free shipping back to Amazon, right? Exactly.</p>\n<p>3. Resellers are selling potentially defective Amazon returns.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.forbes.com/sites/kirimasters/2019/05/06/inside-the-world-of-liquidated-amazon-merchandise/#476da0ea7bf8\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Forbes recently shared on this phenomenon. Amazon sells some of this inventory to liquidation buyers by the pallet or truckload. Amazon offers free returns on these products marked as “defective,” so oftentimes consumers mark products as defective that are in working condition. The result? Resellers like Connelly list these former undesirables with sometimes zero refurbishing in “used” condition. </a></p>\n<p><img decoding=\"async\" class=\"alignright\" style=\"text-align: right;\" src=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/LTSC-3-Amazon-Moves-You-Need-to-Know-About-Now-and-How-You-Can-Compete-3.png\" width=\"378\" height=\"503\" alt=\"\" title=\"\"></p>\n<p>How can you compete? How are you repurposing or reselling returned items? Reselling may not always be the answer, but there is an option that Amazon doesn’t rely on frequently, evidenced by articles like the Rolling Stone’s titled: Jeff Bezos, Amazon: Why ‘Charity’ Is Wrong Solution.</p>\n<p>There has been a lot of dialogue buzzing online about the lack of philanthropy from the eCommerce leader. <a href=\"https://www.vox.com/2018/9/13/17855950/jeff-bezos-donation-2-billion-philanthropy-charity-amazon-ceo\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Vox</a> reported last fall that “scrutiny is not going to end for the world’s wealthiest person, who on Thursday announced he would dedicate at least $2 billion to philanthropic projects. It’s a long time coming for the Amazon CEO, who had yet to spend any real amount of his $163 billion in assets on charity, despite external pressure.”</p>\n<p>There has been a lot of dialogue buzzing online about the lack of philanthropy from the eCommerce leader. Vox reported last fall that “scrutiny is not going to end for the world’s wealthiest person, who on Thursday announced he would <a href=\"https://twitter.com/JeffBezos/status/1040253796293795842\" target=\"_top\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">dedicate at least $2 billion to philanthropic projects</a>. It’s a long time coming for the Amazon CEO, who had yet to spend any real amount of his $163 billion in assets on charity, despite external pressure.”</p>\n<p>Why not repurpose returns that can’t be marked down and are in working condition to give back to shelters and charities across the community? You’ll keep your margins tighter with tax deductions, but also you’ll also be giving back and keeping an active dialogue going around something that Amazon seems to miss – values and community.</p>\n<p>About The Author:</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" decoding=\"async\" class=\"alignleft\" style=\"text-align: left;\" src=\"https://letstalksupplychain.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/11/LTSC-3-Amazon-Moves-You-Need-to-Know-About-Now-and-How-You-Can-Compete-author.jpg\" width=\"292\" height=\"292\" alt=\"\" title=\"\"></p>\n<p>Naomi Garnice has 13 years of experience in telling brand stories and increasing online lead gen, and exposure and five years of experience managing and mentoring up-and-comers. When she is not at work or at a dog park, Naomi volunteers on the board for the Phoenix American Marketing Association and writes about professional development. Naomi&#8217;s articles have appeared on Mashable and Forbes.com and have been plugged by the New York Times online.</p>\n</div>\n",

    "title": "Top 10 ways to manage through stress",
    "slug": "top-10-ways-to-manage-through-stress",
    "date": "2019-05-02T21:37:40",

    "web_content": "<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>&#8230;and be your best self</p>\n<p>I don&#8217;t know about you but the word &#8220;busy&#8221; is like nails scratching a blackboard for me, some use it instead of saying no to something, others see it as something to be proud of and self-importance. We all have busy in our lives and if we don&#8217;t take care of ourselves it can often leads to exhaustion and stress which are harmful to our minds, bodies, spirit and success.</p>\n<p>I thought I would share with you some of the ways I take a moment to &#8220;un-busy&#8221; and take the stress out of my life. I am not perfect and some days I need a real kick in the ass to put them into action but knowing they are tools in my toolbox brings a sigh of relief.</p>\n<ol>\n<li style=\"list-style-type: none;\">\n<ol>\n<li>Box Breathing &#8211; Breathe in for a count of 4, hold your breath for a count of 4, exhale for a count of 4 and hold that for a count of 4. If you feel anxious before starting as you are doing the exercise, tell yourself that you are safe, in a safe place and nothing can harm you.</li>\n<li>Meditation &#8211; No its not just a fad, no you don&#8217;t have to sit cross legged, palms up and hum (you can if you want). Through meditation some people can bring their heart rate and their bodies to a calm state but everyone has their OWN experience. Some days I do a body scan to get started because I need a focus &#8211; I start at the top of my head and work my way down acknowledging every body part, some days it just takes breathing and going into a meditative state, some times I visualize what I want for my life but trust me it didn&#8217;t come easy. It took years of frustration, patience and a little help from an app called &#8220;headspace&#8221; but once I got it, I got it and it looks different every time. A similar type of meditation is called &#8220;tapping&#8221; that one I am still trying to wrap my head around, but one of these days it will be another tool in the <a style=\"border: none; color: #333; font-weight: normal !important; text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://mexicaninsurance.com/mexico-car-auto-insurance-san-diego-mexican\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" target=\"_blank\">mexicaninsurance.com</a> toolbox.</li>\n<li>Gratitude Journal &#8211; Lets face it, you cant stay in a negative space if you are grateful. Some do this first thing in the morning before they start work, they write down 10 things they are grateful for: my family, the breath I am taking this morning, opportunity, dogs, house (roof over my head) etc. Me? I like to do it before bed &#8211; 3 things I am grateful for that day, 3 things that brought me joy, 3 things that are positive about tomorrow and then sometimes I write my feelings in a feelings journal. (Ok that might feel a little weird for some but that is where I get out the negative and reflect on why I am feeling that way)</li>\n<li>Exercise! &#8211; Take a walk, go to the gym, play a sport, stretch, play with your kids &#8211; get out an do something physical, you will feel so much better. I could be having the worst day but when I put on the catcher&#8217;s equipment and get out on the ball field I feel instantly better.</li>\n<li>Do something you enjoy &#8211; Whatever that is, just make time for it, plan it into your day if you have to.</li>\n<li>Pets &#8211; If you have a pet or your friend has a pet, spread some love and spend sometime with them &#8211; playing with a toy, catching a cuddle or even having a one sided conversation with them</li>\n</ol>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p>Vacation &#8211; Virtual or reality &#8211; Take some time, you don&#8217;t have to go far or spend a lot of money but get out of your regular environment and explore. For me you will catch me on a beach, it is my #1 place to really relax.<a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/sherihinish/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\"> Sheri Hinish </a>recently posted about taking a virtual vacation or using VR to help meditate, I haven&#8217;t tried it yet but I will because if VR can put me on a beach without actually getting on a plane I will be at the beach more often!</p>\n<ol>\n<li>Get Grounded &#8211; preferably in nature but you can do this in your office or at home, just sit in the peace and quiet and just be</li>\n<li>Spa Day &#8211; Book that massage or reflexology appointment and get your relax on!</li>\n<li>Therapy &#8211; Book an appointment with a therapist, I don&#8217;t know about you but man do I get into my own head sometimes and the only way I can untangle and make sense of it all is to go and talk it out with my therapist. Its a new adventure every time! Seriously though I would highly recommend this to anyone and I am not shy to say that I have had one off and on my whole life and it has made a world of difference for me personally and for the people around me.</li>\n</ol>\n<p>Other thoughts: Get your health in order and see a Naturopath that specializes in functional medicine, like mine Dr Callum Cowen of <a href=\"http://phenomhpm.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Phenom HPM</a> He was also on season 1 of the show talking about cortisol and how it can affect you or spend time finding your purpose and spend more time on that.</p>\n<p>In the end, its all about living your best life and being your best self no matter what that looks like for you. Nobody is perfect, especially me but as long as you keep trying no one can hold you back.</p>\n",

    "title": "Have an Interview? Presentation Matters!",
    "slug": "have-an-interview-presentation-matters",
    "date": "2019-04-25T16:24:34",
    "summary": null,
    "main_points": null,

    "web_content": "<p>&#8220;The average person puts only 25% of his energy into his work.The world takes off its hat to those who put in more than 50% of their capacity,and stands on its head for those few and far between souls who devote 100%.&#8221;</p>\n<p>—Andrew Carnegie<br />\nIt’s no secret that I love podcasts, and recently I started to listen to Barbara Corcoran&#8217;s Business Unusual podcast. They are short, to the point and give great bite size takeaways for everyone to turn into action right away. I have been having a lot of conversations around supply chain talent but not enough around interview etiquette, how someone walks into a room or presents themselves in the interview absolutely matters so that is why this particular advice resonated with me and I want to share with the community. Plus when we know better we do better, we change our lives and the journey that we are on and just simply because I think it’s better to win together and spread the knowledge as there might be one person out there who needs to hear it.</p>\n<p>Getting a job in any field is a challenge, but getting a job in supply chain is tough because everything is changing so fast and there is an art to giving a good interview. I recently read a post on Linkedin that asked why we make candidates jump through hoops and go above and beyond when we could just keep it simple. I think it’s on both parties to keep it mindful (unbiased), a meaningful experience and respectful so here are some of the tips Barbara shared on her <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9ObiJKbg0jY\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\">episode </a></p>\n<p>Barbara says&#8230;..Presentation matters!</p>\n<p>#1 BE AWARE of posture when you walk in, this will determine whether you look secure and confident. Barbara says she eliminates 2 out of 3 candidates based on this one alone!</p>\n<p>#2 PRACTICE your handshake&#8230;make sure it is firm and make contact with the inner part of the thumb, push gently. Barbara says if you don&#8217;t do this that it means your untrustworthy &#8211; who knew!</p>\n<p>#3 ALWAYS look into the interviewers eyes because it creates trust &#8211; love this one and I have been practicing this for years, just try not to make it creepy!</p>\n<p>#4 DRESS IN YOUR SUNDAY BEST &#8211; Look respectable which means looking neat and well dressed without attracting attention. For women Barbara says NOT to wear 4in heels, you want to wear shoes that suggest you can work and you can’t work in 4in heels &#8211; #truth</p>\n",
